SELECT TOP(@__p_1) [a].[Id], [a].[CreationTime], [a].[CreatorUserId], [a].[IsAbandoned], [a].[JobArgs], [a].[JobType], [a].[LastTryTime], [a].[NextTryTime], [a].[Priority], [a].[TryCount]
